msg:Bring your child to stay on April 23, 2022, and share your stay experience during the epidemic:
advantage:
1. The room is super large, 120 square meters, and the space is second to the Ritz-Carlton opposite the same price.
2. There is a kitchen - this facility is particularly important during the epidemic, and rice cookers, ovens, pots, knives, and tableware are readily available. You only need to bring ingredients, and there is a large refrigerator.
3. The hotel has a private garden with an elegant environment, with water, rockeries and pavilions. The main reason is that there are almost no people (the reason for not being outside). During the epidemic, you can take off your mask and enjoy the outdoors, and it is rare in this kind of location.
4. Free parking, you can enter and exit freely after checking in and reporting the license plate number at the front desk, and there are sufficient parking spaces (shared parking lot with SKP-S)
5. The TV programs are rich, and the major radio stations in the world are basically covered. The first few channels are CNN, NBC, NHK, Singapore CNA, Phoenix Satellite TV, etc. The last is CCTV.
6. The service attitude is good. All the staff meet and greet each other, and see a child who sent a fruit. Booking from Ctrip is not unwelcome as stated in the previous message.
insufficient:
1. There is a lack of swimming pool, but there is a gym. I only visited it. It is located on the 37th-38th floor of Unit 4. It is a little small, but the scenery outside the window is very good.
2. The apar**ent is divided into 4 units. The breakfast is located on the 40th floor of the 4th unit. I live on the 24th floor of the 1st unit. It is a little tossing to eat breakfast.
In general, it is not allowed to go out of Beijing during the epidemic, and a new environment is needed during the holidays. It is highly recommended to stay here.
